Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 044, the original release, though not the final mission release, of the Apollo 10 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Comanche 051 previously reconstructed from a digitized copy of Comanche 055. The code was then updated by undoing changes made between revisions 044 and 051. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021153D. While there is thus a high degree of confidence in the reconstructed code, there are nevertheless a few changes that remain open to question, particularly in log section P20-P25, though even if these eventually prove incorrect they should not adversely affect code execution. Note also that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Comanche 055 printout, although the added code would likely have changed page numbers for a real Comanche 044 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

001540,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001541,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001542,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Comanche revision 044.
001543,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
001544,000006:                                                                                                  ##              original release of the flight software for the Command
001545,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10.
001546,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Comanche 055. It
001547,000009:                                                                                                  ##              has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
001548,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Comanche 44 in NASA drawing
001549,000011:                                                                                                  ##              2021153D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
001550,000012:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
001551,000013:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001552,000014:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001553,000015:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001554,000016:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-12-03 MAS  Created from Comanche 51.
001555,000017:                                                                                                  ##              2020-12-05 MAS  Removed definitions of EK2VAL, EK3VAL, and
001556,000018:                                                                                                  ##                              STARSAV3.

001559,000021:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001560,000022: 
001561,000023:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001562,000024:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001563,000025:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001564,000026: 
001565,000027:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001566,000028:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001567,000029:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001568,000030: 
001569,000031:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001570,000032:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001571,000033:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001572,000034: 
001573,000035:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001574,000036:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001575,000037: 
001576,000038:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001577,000039: 
001578,000040:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001579,000041:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001580,000042: 
001581,000043:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001582,000044: 
001583,000045:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001584,000046:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001585,000047: 
001586,000048:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001587,000049:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001588,000050:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001589,000051:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001590,000052:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001591,000053:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001592,000054: 
001593,000055:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001594,000056: 
001595,000057:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001596,000058:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001597,000059:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001598,000060:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001599,000061:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001600,000062:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001601,000063:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001602,000064:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001603,000065:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001604,000066:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001605,000067:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 38 

001607,000069:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001608,000070:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001609,000071:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001610,000072:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001611,000073:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001612,000074:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001613,000075:

001616,000078:                                                                                                  #  SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001617,000079: 
001618,000080: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001619,000081: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001620,000082: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001621,000083: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001622,000084: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001623,000085: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001624,000086: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001625,000087:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001626,000088: 
001627,000089: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001628,000090: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001629,000091: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001630,000092: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001631,000093: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001632,000094: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001633,000095: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001634,000096: 
001635,000097: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20                                    
001636,000098: 37,2001                        SR                 EQUALS   21                                    
001637,000099: 37,2001                        CYL                EQUALS   22                                    
001638,000100: 37,2001                        EDOP               EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.
001639,000101: 
001640,000102: 37,2001                        TIME2              EQUALS   24                                    
001641,000103: 37,2001                        TIME1              EQUALS   25                                    
001642,000104: 37,2001                        TIME3              EQUALS   26                                    
001643,000105: 37,2001                        TIME4              EQUALS   27                                    
001644,000106: 37,2001                        TIME5              EQUALS   30                                    
001645,000107: 37,2001                        TIME6              EQUALS   31                                    
001646,000108: 37,2001                        CDUX               EQUALS   32                                    
001647,000109: 37,2001                        CDUY               EQUALS   33                                    
001648,000110: 37,2001                        CDUZ               EQUALS   34                                    
001649,000111: 37,2001                        CDUT               EQUALS   35                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION CDU (WAS OPTY).
001650,000112: 37,2001  0000035               OPTY               =        CDUT                                  
001651,000113: 37,2001                        CDUS               EQUALS   36                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT CDU (WAS OPTX).
001652,000114: 37,2001  0000036               OPTX               =        CDUS                                  
001653,000115: 37,2001                        PIPAX              EQUALS   37                                    
001654,000116: 37,2001                        PIPAY              EQUALS   40                                    
001655,000117: 37,2001                        PIPAZ              EQUALS   41                                    
001656,000118: 37,2001                        BMAGX              EQUALS   42                                    
001657,000119: 37,2001                        BMAGY              EQUALS   43                                    
001658,000120: 37,2001                        BMAGZ              EQUALS   44                                    
001659,000121: 37,2001                        INLINK             EQUALS   45                                    
001660,000122: 37,2001                        RNRAD              EQUALS   46                                    
001661,000123: 37,2001                        GYROCTR            EQUALS   47                                    
001662,000124: 37,2001                        GYROCMD            EQUALS   47                                    
001663,000125: 37,2001                        CDUXCMD            EQUALS   50                                    
001664,000126: 37,2001                        CDUYCMD            EQUALS   51

001669,000131: 37,2001                        CDUTCMD            EQUALS   53                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION COMMAND (WAS OPTYCMD).
001670,000132: 37,2001  0000053               OPTYCMD            =        CDUTCMD                               
001671,000133: 37,2001  0000053               TVCYAW             EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE.

001673,000135: 37,2001  0000054               TVCPITCH           EQUALS   CDUSCMD                               #  SPS PITCH COMMAND IN TVC MODE.

001686,000148: 37,2001                        X2                 EQUALS   39D                                   #  TO THE WORK AREA.
